<p><strong>What are two responsibilities that you will have as a British citizen or permanent resident of the UK?</strong></p>
                            </div>

                                            <label>
                                                <input class="wpProQuiz_questionInput"
                                                       type="checkbox"
                                                       name="question_82_4657"
                                                       value="1"> To look after the area in which you live and the environment                                            </label>

                                                                            </li>
                                    
                                    <li class="wpProQuiz_questionListItem" data-pos="1">

                                            <label>
                                                <input class="wpProQuiz_questionInput"

                                                       name="question_82_4657"

                                                                            </li>

                                            <label>

                                    <p></p>                                </div>

                                                                            <span class="wpProQuiz_respone_span">
									Incorrect								</span><br>
                                    <p>If you wish to be a permanent resident or citizen of the UK, you should: <strong>look after yourself and your family, look after the area in which you live and the environment</strong>, respect and obey the law, respect the rights of others, including their right to their own opinions and treat others with fairness.</p>

								                function readCookie(name) {
                                                    var nameEQ = name + "=";
                                                    var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
                                                    for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) { var c = ca[i]; while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length); if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length); } return null; }

												<p>Passed my test yesterday in Croydon!</p>
<p>19 questions were from exams1-16 and 3 new ones related the location of Skara Brae (Scotland), one related which church Scotland followed in a specific year (don’t remember exactly) and I don’t remember the last one, sorry!</p>
<p>My advice is to study carefully all the 16 exams, both answers and questions because at the exam they are not exactly the same as here, but if you practice the 16 exams you can answer them all!</p>
<p>Good luck everyone!</p>

They register anonymous statistical data on for example how many times the video is displayed and what settings are used for playback.No sensitive data is collected unless you log in to your google account, in that case your choices are linked with your account, for example if you click “like” on a video.</td></tr></tbody></table></div>
